histograms[:n+1]\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\thistograms = append(histograms, HPoint{H: &histogram.FloatHistogram{}})\n\t\t}\n\t\tif histograms[n].H == nil {\n\t\t\t// Make sure to pass non-nil H to AtFloatHistogram so that it does a deep-copy.\n\t\t\t// Not an issue in the loop above since that uses an intermediate buffer.\n\t\t\thistograms[n].H = &histogram.FloatHistogram{}\n\t\t}\n\t\thistograms[n].T, histograms[n].H = it.AtFloatHistogram(histograms[n].H)\n\t\tif value.IsStaleNaN(histograms[n].H.Sum) {\n\t\t\thistograms = histograms[:n]\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tev.currentSamples += histograms[n].size()\n\t\tif ev.currentSamples > ev.maxSamples {\n\t\t\tev.error(ErrTooManySamples(env))\n\t\t}\n\n\tcase chunkenc.ValFloat:\n\t\tt, f := it.At()\n\t\tif t == maxt && !value.IsStaleNaN(f) {\n\t\t\tev.currentSamples++\n\t\t\tif ev.currentSamples > ev.maxSamples {\n\t\t\t\tev.error(ErrTooManySamples(env))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif floats == nil {\n\t\t\t\tfloats = getFPointSlice(16)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfloats = append(floats, FPoint{T: t, F: f})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tev.samplesStats.UpdatePeak(ev.currentSamples)\n\treturn floats, histograms\n}\n\nfunc (*evaluator) VectorAnd(lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper) Vector {\n\tif matching.Card != parser.CardManyToMany {\n\t\tpanic(\"set operations must only use many-to-many matching\")\n\t}\n\tif len(lhs) == 0 || len(rhs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil // Short-circuit: AND with nothing is nothing.\n\t}\n\n\t// The set of signatures for the right-hand side Vector.\n\trightSigs := map[string]struct{}{}\n\t// Add all rhs samples to a map so we can easily find matches later.\n\tfor _, sh := range rhsh {\n\t\trightSigs[sh.signature] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\t// If there's a matching entry in the right-hand side Vector, add the sample.\n\t\tif _, ok := rightSigs[lhsh[i].signature]; ok {\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, ls)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out\n}\n\nfunc (*evaluator) VectorOr(lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper) Vector {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase matching.Card != parser.CardManyToMany:\n\t\tpanic(\"set operations must only use many-to-many matching\")\n\tcase len(lhs) == 0: // Short-circuit.\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, rhs...)\n\t\treturn enh.Out\n\tcase len(rhs) == 0:\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, lhs...)\n\t\treturn enh.Out\n\t}\n\n\tleftSigs := map[string]struct{}{}\n\t// Add everything from the left-hand-side Vector.\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\tleftSigs[lhsh[i].signature] = struct{}{}\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, ls)\n\t}\n\t// Add all right-hand side elements which have not been added from the left-hand side.\n\tfor j, rs := range rhs {\n\t\tif _, ok := leftSigs[rhsh[j].signature]; !ok {\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, rs)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out\n}\n\nfunc (*evaluator) VectorUnless(lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper) Vector {\n\tif matching.Card != parser.CardManyToMany {\n\t\tpanic(\"set operations must only use many-to-many matching\")\n\t}\n\t// Short-circuit: empty rhs means we will return everything in lhs;\n\t// empty lhs means we will return empty - don't need to build a map.\n\tif len(lhs) == 0 || len(rhs) == 0 {\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, lhs...)\n\t\treturn enh.Out\n\t}\n\n\trightSigs := map[string]struct{}{}\n\tfor _, sh := range rhsh {\n\t\trightSigs[sh.signature] = struct{}{}\n\t}\n\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\tif _, ok := rightSigs[lhsh[i].signature]; !ok {\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, ls)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out\n}\n\n// VectorBinop evaluates a binary operation between two Vectors, excluding set operators.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) VectorBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs, rhs Vector, matching *parser.VectorMatching, returnBool bool, lhsh, rhsh []EvalSeriesHelper, enh *EvalNodeHelper, pos posrange.PositionRange) (Vector, error) {\n\tif matching.Card == parser.CardManyToMany {\n\t\tpanic(\"many-to-many only allowed for set operators\")\n\t}\n\tif len(lhs) == 0 || len(rhs) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil, nil // Short-circuit: nothing is going to match.\n\t}\n\n\t// The control flow below handles one-to-one or many-to-one matching.\n\t// For one-to-many, swap sidedness and account for the swap when calculating\n\t// values.\n\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToMany {\n\t\tlhs, rhs = rhs, lhs\n\t\tlhsh, rhsh = rhsh, lhsh\n\t}\n\n\t// All samples from the rhs hashed by the matching label/values.\n\tif enh.rightSigs == nil {\n\t\tenh.rightSigs = make(map[string]Sample, len(enh.Out))\n\t} else {\n\t\tfor k := range enh.rightSigs {\n\t\t\tdelete(enh.rightSigs, k)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trightSigs := enh.rightSigs\n\n\t// Add all rhs samples to a map so we can easily find matches later.\n\tfor i, rs := range rhs {\n\t\tsig := rhsh[i].signature\n\t\t// The rhs is guaranteed to be the 'one' side. Having multiple samples\n\t\t// with the same signature means that the matching is many-to-many.\n\t\tif duplSample, found := rightSigs[sig]; found {\n\t\t\t// oneSide represents which side of the vector represents the 'one' in the many-to-one relationship.\n\t\t\toneSide := \"right\"\n\t\t\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToMany {\n\t\t\t\toneSide = \"left\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tmatchedLabels := rs.Metric.MatchLabels(matching.On, matching.MatchingLabels...)\n\t\t\t// Many-to-many matching not allowed.\n\t\t\tev.errorf(\"found duplicate series for the match group %s on the %s hand-side of the operation: [%s, %s]\"+\n\t\t\t\t\";many-to-many matching not allowed: matching labels must be unique on one side\", matchedLabels.String(), oneSide, rs.Metric.String(), duplSample.Metric.String())\n\t\t}\n\t\trightSigs[sig] = rs\n\t}\n\n\t// Tracks the match-signature. For one-to-one operations the value is nil. For many-to-one\n\t// the value is a set of signatures to detect duplicated result elements.\n\tif enh.matchedSigs == nil {\n\t\tenh.matchedSigs = make(map[string]map[uint64]struct{}, len(rightSigs))\n\t} else {\n\t\tfor k := range enh.matchedSigs {\n\t\t\tdelete(enh.matchedSigs, k)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tmatchedSigs := enh.matchedSigs\n\n\t// For all lhs samples find a respective rhs sample and perform\n\t// the binary operation.\n\tvar lastErr error\n\tfor i, ls := range lhs {\n\t\tsig := lhsh[i].signature\n\n\t\trs, found := rightSigs[sig] // Look for a match in the rhs Vector.\n\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Account for potentially swapped sidedness.\n\t\tfl, fr := ls.F, rs.F\n\t\thl, hr := ls.H, rs.H\n\t\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToMany {\n\t\t\tfl, fr = fr, fl\n\t\t\thl, hr = hr, hl\n\t\t}\n\t\tfloatValue, histogramValue, keep, err := vectorElemBinop(op, fl, fr, hl, hr, pos)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlastErr = err\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase returnBool:\n\t\t\thistogramValue = nil\n\t\t\tif keep {\n\t\t\t\tfloatValue = 1.0\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tfloatValue = 0.0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase !keep:\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetric := resultMetric(ls.Metric, rs.Metric, op, matching, enh)\n\t\tif !ev.enableDelayedNameRemoval && returnBool {\n\t\t\tmetric = metric.DropReserved(schema.IsMetadataLabel)\n\t\t}\n\t\tinsertedSigs, exists := matchedSigs[sig]\n\t\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToOne {\n\t\t\tif exists {\n\t\t\t\tev.errorf(\"multiple matches for labels: many-to-one matching must be explicit (group_left/group_right)\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tmatchedSigs[sig] = nil // Set existence to true.\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// In many-to-one matching the grouping labels have to ensure a unique metric\n\t\t\t// for the result Vector. Check whether those labels have already been added for\n\t\t\t// the same matching labels.\n\t\t\tinsertSig := metric.Hash()\n\n\t\t\tif !exists {\n\t\t\t\tinsertedSigs = map[uint64]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\tmatchedSigs[sig] = insertedSigs\n\t\t\t} else if _, duplicate := insertedSigs[insertSig]; duplicate {\n\t\t\t\tev.errorf(\"multiple matches for labels: grouping labels must ensure unique matches\")\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tinsertedSigs[insertSig] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, Sample{\n\t\t\tMetric:   metric,\n\t\t\tF:        floatValue,\n\t\t\tH:        histogramValue,\n\t\t\tDropName: returnBool,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out, lastErr\n}\n\nfunc signatureFunc(on bool, b []byte, names ...string) func(labels.Labels) string {\n\tif on {\n\t\tslices.Sort(names)\n\t\treturn func(lset labels.Labels) string {\n\t\t\treturn string(lset.BytesWithLabels(b, names...))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tnames = append([]string{labels.MetricName}, names...)\n\tslices.Sort(names)\n\treturn func(lset labels.Labels) string {\n\t\treturn string(lset.BytesWithoutLabels(b, names...))\n\t}\n}\n\n// resultMetric returns the metric for the given sample(s) based on the Vector\n// binary operation and the matching options.\nfunc resultMetric(lhs, rhs labels.Labels, op parser.ItemType, matching *parser.VectorMatching, enh *EvalNodeHelper) labels.Labels {\n\tif enh.resultMetric == nil {\n\t\tenh.resultMetric = make(map[string]labels.Labels, len(enh.Out))\n\t}\n\n\tenh.resetBuilder(lhs)\n\tbuf := bytes.NewBuffer(enh.lblResultBuf[:0])\n\tenh.lblBuf = lhs.Bytes(enh.lblBuf)\n\tbuf.Write(enh.lblBuf)\n\tenh.lblBuf = rhs.Bytes(enh.lblBuf)\n\tbuf.Write(enh.lblBuf)\n\tenh.lblResultBuf = buf.Bytes()\n\n\tif ret, ok := enh.resultMetric[string(enh.lblResultBuf)]; ok {\n\t\treturn ret\n\t}\n\tstr := string(enh.lblResultBuf)\n\n\tif changesMetricSchema(op) {\n\t\t// Setting empty Metadata causes the deletion of those if they exists.\n\t\tschema.Metadata{}.SetToLabels(enh.lb)\n\t}\n\n\tif matching.Card == parser.CardOneToOne {\n\t\tif matching.On {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Keep(matching.MatchingLabels...)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Del(matching.MatchingLabels...)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, ln := range matching.Include {\n\t\t// Included labels from the `group_x` modifier are taken from the \"one\"-side.\n\t\tif v := rhs.Get(ln); v != \"\" {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Set(ln, v)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Del(ln)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tret := enh.lb.Labels()\n\tenh.resultMetric[str] = ret\n\treturn ret\n}\n\n// VectorscalarBinop evaluates a binary operation between a Vector and a Scalar.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) VectorscalarBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs Vector, rhs Scalar, swap, returnBool bool, enh *EvalNodeHelper, pos posrange.PositionRange) (Vector, error) {\n\tvar lastErr error\n\tfor _, lhsSample := range lhs {\n\t\tlf, rf := lhsSample.F, rhs.V\n\t\tvar rh *histogram.FloatHistogram\n\t\tlh := lhsSample.H\n\t\t// lhs always contains the Vector. If the original position was different\n\t\t// swap for calculating the value.\n\t\tif swap {\n\t\t\tlf, rf = rf, lf\n\t\t\tlh, rh = rh, lh\n\t\t}\n\t\tfloat, histogram, keep, err := vectorElemBinop(op, lf, rf, lh, rh, pos)\n\t\tif err != nil && !errors.Is(err, annotations.PromQLWarning) {\n\t\t\tlastErr = err\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Catch cases where the scalar is the LHS in a scalar-vector comparison operation.\n\t\t// We want to always keep the vector element value as the output value, even if it's on the RHS.\n\t\tif op.IsComparisonOperator() && swap {\n\t\t\tfloat = rf\n\t\t\thistogram = rh\n\t\t}\n\t\tif returnBool {\n\t\t\tif keep {\n\t\t\t\tfloat = 1.0\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tfloat = 0.0\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tkeep = true\n\t\t}\n\t\tif keep {\n\t\t\tlhsSample.F = float\n\t\t\tlhsSample.H = histogram\n\t\t\tif changesMetricSchema(op) || returnBool {\n\t\t\t\tif !ev.enableDelayedNameRemoval {\n\t\t\t\t\tlhsSample.Metric = lhsSample.Metric.DropReserved(schema.IsMetadataLabel)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tlhsSample.DropName = true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tenh.Out = append(enh.Out, lhsSample)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn enh.Out, lastErr\n}\n\n// scalarBinop evaluates a binary operation between two Scalars.\nfunc scalarBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs, rhs float64) float64 {\n\tswitch op {\n\tcase parser.ADD:\n\t\treturn lhs + rhs\n\tcase parser.SUB:\n\t\treturn lhs - rhs\n\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\treturn lhs * rhs\n\tcase parser.DIV:\n\t\treturn lhs / rhs\n\tcase parser.POW:\n\t\treturn math.Pow(lhs, rhs)\n\tcase parser.MOD:\n\t\treturn math.Mod(lhs, rhs)\n\tcase parser.EQLC:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs == rhs)\n\tcase parser.NEQ:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs != rhs)\n\tcase parser.GTR:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs > rhs)\n\tcase parser.LSS:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs < rhs)\n\tcase parser.GTE:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs >= rhs)\n\tcase parser.LTE:\n\t\treturn btos(lhs <= rhs)\n\tcase parser.ATAN2:\n\t\treturn math.Atan2(lhs, rhs)\n\t}\n\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"operator %q not allowed for Scalar operations\", op))\n}\n\n// vectorElemBinop evaluates a binary operation between two Vector elements.\nfunc vectorElemBinop(op parser.ItemType, lhs, rhs float64, hlhs, hrhs *histogram.FloatHistogram, pos posrange.PositionRange) (float64, *histogram.FloatHistogram, bool, error) {\n\topName := parser.ItemTypeStr[op]\n\tswitch {\n\tcase hlhs == nil && hrhs == nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs + rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.SUB:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs - rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs * rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.DIV:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs / rhs, nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.POW:\n\t\t\t\treturn math.Pow(lhs, rhs), nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.MOD:\n\t\t\t\treturn math.Mod(lhs, rhs), nil, true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.EQLC:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs == rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.NEQ:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs != rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.GTR:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs > rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.LSS:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs < rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.GTE:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs >= rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.LTE:\n\t\t\t\treturn lhs, nil, lhs <= rhs, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn math.Atan2(lhs, rhs), nil, true, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase hlhs == nil && hrhs != nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hrhs.Copy().Mul(lhs).Compact(0), true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD, parser.SUB, parser.DIV, parser.POW, parser.MOD, parser.EQLC, parser.NEQ, parser.GTR, parser.LSS, parser.GTE, parser.LTE, parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, annotations.NewIncompatibleTypesInBinOpInfo(\"float\", opName, \"histogram\", pos)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase hlhs != nil && hrhs == nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs.Copy().Mul(rhs).Compact(0), true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.DIV:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs.Copy().Div(rhs).Compact(0), true, nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD, parser.SUB, parser.POW, parser.MOD, parser.EQLC, parser.NEQ, parser.GTR, parser.LSS, parser.GTE, parser.LTE, parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, annotations.NewIncompatibleTypesInBinOpInfo(\"histogram\", opName, \"float\", pos)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\tcase hlhs != nil && hrhs != nil:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.ADD:\n\t\t\t\tres, counterResetCollision, err := hlhs.Copy().Add(hrhs)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif counterResetCollision {\n\t\t\t\t\terr = annotations.NewHistogramCounterResetCollisionWarning(pos, annotations.HistogramAdd)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, res.Compact(0), true, err\n\t\t\tcase parser.SUB:\n\t\t\t\tres, counterResetCollision, err := hlhs.Copy().Sub(hrhs)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif counterResetCollision {\n\t\t\t\t\terr = annotations.NewHistogramCounterResetCollisionWarning(pos, annotations.HistogramSub)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, res.Compact(0), true, err\n\t\t\tcase parser.EQLC:\n\t\t\t\t// This operation expects that both histograms are compacted.\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs, hlhs.Equals(hrhs), nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.NEQ:\n\t\t\t\t// This operation expects that both histograms are compacted.\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, hlhs, !hlhs.Equals(hrhs), nil\n\t\t\tcase parser.MUL, parser.DIV, parser.POW, parser.MOD, parser.GTR, parser.LSS, parser.GTE, parser.LTE, parser.ATAN2:\n\t\t\t\treturn 0, nil, false, annotations.NewIncompatibleTypesInBinOpInfo(\"histogram\", opName, \"histogram\", pos)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"operator %q not allowed for operations between Vectors\", op))\n}\n\ntype groupedAggregation struct {\n\tfloatValue     float64\n\thistogramValue *histogram.FloatHistogram\n\tfloatMean      float64\n\tfloatKahanC    float64 // \"Compensating value\" for Kahan summation.\n\tgroupCount     float64\n\theap           vectorByValueHeap\n\n\t// All bools together for better packing within the struct.\n\tseen                   bool // Was this output groups seen in the input at this timestamp.\n\thasFloat               bool // Has at least 1 float64 sample aggregated.\n\thasHistogram           bool // Has at least 1 histogram sample aggregated.\n\tincompatibleHistograms bool // If true, group has seen mixed exponential and custom buckets, or incompatible custom buckets.\n\tgroupAggrComplete      bool // Used by LIMITK to short-cut series loop when we've reached K elem on every group.\n\tincrementalMean        bool // True after reverting to incremental calculation of the mean value.\n}\n\n// aggregation evaluates sum, avg, count, stdvar, stddev or quantile at one timestep on inputMatrix.\n// These functions produce one output series for each group specified in the expression, with just the labels from `by(...)`.\n// outputMatrix should be already populated with grouping labels; groups is one-to-one with outputMatrix.\n// seriesToResult maps inputMatrix indexes to outputMatrix indexes.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) aggregation(e *parser.AggregateExpr, q float64, inputMatrix, outputMatrix Matrix, seriesToResult []int, groups []groupedAggregation, enh *EvalNodeHelper) annotations.Annotations {\n\top := e.Op\n\tvar annos annotations.Annotations\n\tfor i := range groups {\n\t\tgroups[i].seen = false\n\t}\n\n\tfor si := range inputMatrix {\n\t\tf, h, ok := ev.nextValues(enh.Ts, &inputMatrix[si])\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tgroup := &groups[seriesToResult[si]]\n\t\t// Initialize this group if it's the first time we've seen it.\n\t\tif !group.seen {\n\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\tseen:                   true,\n\t\t\t\tfloatValue:             f,\n\t\t\t\tfloatMean:              f,\n\t\t\t\tincompatibleHistograms: false,\n\t\t\t\tgroupCount:             1,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.AVG, parser.SUM:\n\t\t\t\tif h == nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.hasFloat = true\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.histogramValue = h.Copy()\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.hasHistogram = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.STDVAR, parser.STDDEV:\n\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\tcase h != nil:\n\t\t\t\t\t// Ignore histograms for STDVAR and STDDEV.\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tif op == parser.STDVAR {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stdvar\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stddev\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcase math.IsNaN(f), math.IsInf(f, 0):\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = math.NaN()\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = 0\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.QUANTILE:\n\t\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"quantile\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap = make(vectorByValueHeap, 1)\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = Sample{F: f}\n\t\t\tcase parser.GROUP:\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = 1\n\t\t\tcase parser.MIN, parser.MAX:\n\t\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tif op == parser.MIN {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"min\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"max\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif group.incompatibleHistograms {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.SUM:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasHistogram = true\n\t\t\t\tif group.histogramValue != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t_, _, err := group.histogramValue.Add(h)\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\thandleAggregationError(err, e, inputMatrix[si].Metric.Get(model.MetricNameLabel), &annos)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incompatibleHistograms = true\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise the aggregation contained floats\n\t\t\t\t// previously and will be invalid anyway. No\n\t\t\t\t// point in copying the histogram in that case.\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasFloat = true\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue, group.floatKahanC = kahanSumInc(f, group.floatValue, group.floatKahanC)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.AVG:\n\t\t\t// For the average calculation of histograms, we use\n\t\t\t// incremental mean calculation without the help of\n\t\t\t// Kahan summation (but this should change, see\n\t\t\t// https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/14105\n\t\t\t// ). For floats, we improve the accuracy with the help\n\t\t\t// of Kahan summation. For a while, we assumed that\n\t\t\t// incremental mean calculation combined with Kahan\n\t\t\t// summation (see\n\t\t\t// https://stackoverflow.com/questions/61665473/is-it-beneficial-for-precision-to-calculate-the-incremental-mean-average\n\t\t\t// for inspiration) is generally the preferred solution.\n\t\t\t// However, it then turned out that direct mean\n\t\t\t// calculation (still in combination with Kahan\n\t\t\t// summation) is often more accurate. See discussion in\n\t\t\t// https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/16714\n\t\t\t// . The problem with the direct mean calculation is\n\t\t\t// that it can overflow float64 for inputs on which the\n\t\t\t// incremental mean calculation works just fine. Our\n\t\t\t// current approach is therefore to use direct mean\n\t\t\t// calculation as long as we do not overflow (or\n\t\t\t// underflow) the running sum. Once the latter would\n\t\t\t// happen, we switch to incremental mean calculation.\n\t\t\t// This seems to work reasonably well, but note that a\n\t\t\t// deeper understanding would be needed to find out if\n\t\t\t// maybe an earlier switch to incremental mean\n\t\t\t// calculation would be better in terms of accuracy.\n\t\t\t// Also, we could apply a number of additional means to\n\t\t\t// improve the accuracy, like processing the values in a\n\t\t\t// particular order. For now, we decided that the\n\t\t\t// current implementation is accurate enough for\n\t\t\t// practical purposes, in particular given that changing\n\t\t\t// the order of summation would be hard, given how the\n\t\t\t// PromQL engine implements aggregations.\n\t\t\tgroup.groupCount++\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasHistogram = true\n\t\t\t\tif group.histogramValue != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tleft := h.Copy().Div(group.groupCount)\n\t\t\t\t\tright := group.histogramValue.Copy().Div(group.groupCount)\n\t\t\t\t\ttoAdd, _, err := left.Sub(right)\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\thandleAggregationError(err, e, inputMatrix[si].Metric.Get(model.MetricNameLabel), &annos)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incompatibleHistograms = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t_, _, err = group.histogramValue.Add(toAdd)\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\thandleAggregationError(err, e, inputMatrix[si].Metric.Get(model.MetricNameLabel), &annos)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incompatibleHistograms = true\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise the aggregation contained floats\n\t\t\t\t// previously and will be invalid anyway. No\n\t\t\t\t// point in copying the histogram in that case.\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.hasFloat = true\n\t\t\t\tif !group.incrementalMean {\n\t\t\t\t\tnewV, newC := kahanSumInc(f, group.floatValue, group.floatKahanC)\n\t\t\t\t\tif !math.IsInf(newV, 0) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// The sum doesn't overflow, so we propagate it to the\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// group struct and continue with the regular\n\t\t\t\t\t\t// calculation of the mean value.\n\t\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue, group.floatKahanC = newV, newC\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t// If we are here, we know that the sum _would_ overflow. So\n\t\t\t\t\t// instead of continue to sum up, we revert to incremental\n\t\t\t\t\t// calculation of the mean value from here on.\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.incrementalMean = true\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatMean = group.floatValue / (group.groupCount - 1)\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.floatKahanC /= group.groupCount - 1\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tq := (group.groupCount - 1) / group.groupCount\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatMean, group.floatKahanC = kahanSumInc(\n\t\t\t\t\tf/group.groupCount,\n\t\t\t\t\tq*group.floatMean,\n\t\t\t\t\tq*group.floatKahanC,\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.GROUP:\n\t\t\t// Do nothing. Required to avoid the panic in `default:` below.\n\n\t\tcase parser.MAX:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"max\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif group.floatValue < f || math.IsNaN(group.floatValue) {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = f\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.MIN:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"min\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif group.floatValue > f || math.IsNaN(group.floatValue) {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue = f\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.COUNT:\n\t\t\tgroup.groupCount++\n\n\t\tcase parser.STDVAR, parser.STDDEV:\n\t\t\tif h == nil { // Ignore native histograms.\n\t\t\t\tgroup.groupCount++\n\t\t\t\tdelta := f - group.floatMean\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatMean += delta / group.groupCount\n\t\t\t\tgroup.floatValue += delta * (f - group.floatMean)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tif op == parser.STDVAR {\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stdvar\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"stddev\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.QUANTILE:\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"quantile\", e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tgroup.heap = append(group.heap, Sample{F: f})\n\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"expected aggregation operator but got %q\", op))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the output matrix from the aggregated groups.\n\tnumSteps := int((ev.endTimestamp-ev.startTimestamp)/ev.interval) + 1\n\n\tfor ri, aggr := range groups {\n\t\tif !aggr.seen {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.AVG:\n\t\t\tif aggr.hasFloat && aggr.hasHistogram {\n\t\t\t\t// We cannot aggregate histogram sample with a float64 sample.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewMixedFloatsHistogramsAggWarning(e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase aggr.incompatibleHistograms:\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\tcase aggr.hasHistogram:\n\t\t\t\taggr.histogramValue = aggr.histogramValue.Compact(0)\n\t\t\tcase aggr.incrementalMean:\n\t\t\t\taggr.floatValue = aggr.floatMean + aggr.floatKahanC\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\taggr.floatValue = aggr.floatValue/aggr.groupCount + aggr.floatKahanC/aggr.groupCount\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.COUNT:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue = aggr.groupCount\n\n\t\tcase parser.STDVAR:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue /= aggr.groupCount\n\n\t\tcase parser.STDDEV:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue = math.Sqrt(aggr.floatValue / aggr.groupCount)\n\n\t\tcase parser.QUANTILE:\n\t\t\taggr.floatValue = quantile(q, aggr.heap)\n\n\t\tcase parser.SUM:\n\t\t\tif aggr.hasFloat && aggr.hasHistogram {\n\t\t\t\t// We cannot aggregate histogram sample with a float64 sample.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewMixedFloatsHistogramsAggWarning(e.Expr.PositionRange()))\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase aggr.incompatibleHistograms:\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\tcase aggr.hasHistogram:\n\t\t\t\taggr.histogramValue.Compact(0)\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\taggr.floatValue += aggr.floatKahanC\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t// For other aggregations, we already have the right value.\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tss := &outputMatrix[ri]\n\t\taddToSeries(ss, enh.Ts, aggr.floatValue, aggr.histogramValue, numSteps)\n\t\tss.DropName = inputMatrix[ri].DropName\n\t}\n\n\treturn annos\n}\n\n// aggregationK evaluates topk, bottomk, limitk, or limit_ratio at one timestep on inputMatrix.\n// Output that has the same labels as the input, but just k of them per group.\n// seriesToResult maps inputMatrix indexes to groups indexes.\n// For an instant query, returns a Matrix in descending order for topk or ascending for bottomk, or without any order for limitk / limit_ratio.\n// For a range query, aggregates output in the seriess map.\nfunc (ev *evaluator) aggregationK(e *parser.AggregateExpr, fParam float64, inputMatrix Matrix, seriesToResult []int, groups []groupedAggregation, enh *EvalNodeHelper, seriess map[uint64]Series) (Matrix, annotations.Annotations) {\n\top := e.Op\n\tvar s Sample\n\tvar annos annotations.Annotations\n\t// Used to short-cut the loop for LIMITK if we already collected k elements for every group\n\tgroupsRemaining := len(groups)\n\tfor i := range groups {\n\t\tgroups[i].seen = false\n\t}\n\t// advanceRemainingSeries discards any values at the current timestamp `ts`\n\t// for the remaining input series. In range queries, if these values are not\n\t// consumed now, they will no longer be accessible in the next evaluation step.\n\tadvanceRemainingSeries := func(ts int64, startIdx int) {\n\t\tfor i := startIdx; i < len(inputMatrix); i++ {\n\t\t\t_, _, _ = ev.nextValues(ts, &inputMatrix[i])\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\nseriesLoop:\n\tfor si := range inputMatrix {\n\t\tf, h, ok := ev.nextValues(enh.Ts, &inputMatrix[si])\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\ts = Sample{Metric: inputMatrix[si].Metric, F: f, H: h, DropName: inputMatrix[si].DropName}\n\n\t\tvar k int64\n\t\tvar r float64\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.TOPK, parser.BOTTOMK, parser.LIMITK:\n\t\t\tk = min(int64(fParam), int64(len(inputMatrix)))\n\t\t\tif k < 1 {\n\t\t\t\tif enh.Ts != ev.endTimestamp {\n\t\t\t\t\tadvanceRemainingSeries(enh.Ts, si+1)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, annos\n\t\t\t}\n\t\tcase parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase fParam == 0:\n\t\t\t\tif enh.Ts != ev.endTimestamp {\n\t\t\t\t\tadvanceRemainingSeries(enh.Ts, si+1)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, annos\n\t\t\tcase fParam < -1.0:\n\t\t\t\tr = -1.0\n\t\t\tcase fParam > 1.0:\n\t\t\t\tr = 1.0\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\tr = fParam\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tgroup := &groups[seriesToResult[si]]\n\t\t// Initialize this group if it's the first time we've seen it.\n\t\tif !group.seen {\n\t\t\t// LIMIT_RATIO is a special case, as we may not add this very sample to the heap,\n\t\t\t// while we also don't know the final size of it.\n\t\t\tswitch op {\n\t\t\tcase parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 0),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif ratiosampler.AddRatioSample(r, &s) {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.LIMITK:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 1, k),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = s\n\t\t\tcase parser.TOPK:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 0, k),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif s.H != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"topk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcase parser.BOTTOMK:\n\t\t\t\t*group = groupedAggregation{\n\t\t\t\t\tseen: true,\n\t\t\t\t\theap: make(vectorByValueHeap, 0, k),\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif s.H != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tgroup.seen = false\n\t\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"bottomk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.TOPK:\n\t\t\t// We build a heap of up to k elements, with the smallest element at heap[0].\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase s.H != nil:\n\t\t\t\t// Ignore histogram sample and add info annotation.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"topk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\tcase int64(len(group.heap)) < k:\n\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\tcase group.heap[0].F < s.F || (math.IsNaN(group.heap[0].F) && !math.IsNaN(s.F)):\n\t\t\t\t// This new element is bigger than the previous smallest element - overwrite that.\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = s\n\t\t\t\tif k > 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Fix(&group.heap, 0) // Maintain the heap invariant.\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.BOTTOMK:\n\t\t\t// We build a heap of up to k elements, with the biggest element at heap[0].\n\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\tcase s.H != nil:\n\t\t\t\t// Ignore histogram sample and add info annotation.\n\t\t\t\tannos.Add(annotations.NewHistogramIgnoredInAggregationInfo(\"bottomk\", e.PosRange))\n\t\t\tcase int64(len(group.heap)) < k:\n\t\t\t\theap.Push((*vectorByReverseValueHeap)(&group.heap), &s)\n\t\t\tcase group.heap[0].F > s.F || (math.IsNaN(group.heap[0].F) && !math.IsNaN(s.F)):\n\t\t\t\t// This new element is smaller than the previous biggest element - overwrite that.\n\t\t\t\tgroup.heap[0] = s\n\t\t\t\tif k > 1 {\n\t\t\t\t\theap.Fix((*vectorByReverseValueHeap)(&group.heap), 0) // Maintain the heap invariant.\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.LIMITK:\n\t\t\tif int64(len(group.heap)) < k {\n\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// LIMITK optimization: early break if we've added K elem to _every_ group,\n\t\t\t// especially useful for large timeseries where the user is exploring labels via e.g.\n\t\t\t// limitk(10, my_metric)\n\t\t\tif !group.groupAggrComplete && int64(len(group.heap)) == k {\n\t\t\t\tgroup.groupAggrComplete = true\n\t\t\t\tgroupsRemaining--\n\t\t\t\tif groupsRemaining == 0 {\n\t\t\t\t\t// Process other values in the series before breaking the loop in case of range query.\n\t\t\t\t\tif enh.Ts != ev.endTimestamp {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tadvanceRemainingSeries(enh.Ts, si+1)\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak seriesLoop\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\tif ratiosampler.AddRatioSample(r, &s) {\n\t\t\t\theap.Push(&group.heap, &s)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"expected aggregation operator but got %q\", op))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the result from the aggregated groups.\n\tnumSteps := int((ev.endTimestamp-ev.startTimestamp)/ev.interval) + 1\n\tvar mat Matrix\n\tif ev.endTimestamp == ev.startTimestamp {\n\t\tmat = make(Matrix, 0, len(groups))\n\t}\n\n\tadd := func(lbls labels.Labels, f float64, h *histogram.FloatHistogram, dropName bool) {\n\t\t// If this could be an instant query, add directly to the matrix so the result is in consistent order.\n\t\tif ev.endTimestamp == ev.startTimestamp {\n\t\t\tif h != nil {\n\t\t\t\tmat = append(mat, Series{Metric: lbls, Histograms: []HPoint{{T: enh.Ts, H: h}}, DropName: dropName})\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tmat = append(mat, Series{Metric: lbls, Floats: []FPoint{{T: enh.Ts, F: f}}, DropName: dropName})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// Otherwise the results are added into seriess elements.\n\t\t\thash := lbls.Hash()\n\t\t\tss, ok := seriess[hash]\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tss = Series{Metric: lbls, DropName: dropName}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\taddToSeries(&ss, enh.Ts, f, h, numSteps)\n\t\t\tseriess[hash] = ss\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tfor _, aggr := range groups {\n\t\tif !aggr.seen {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tswitch op {\n\t\tcase parser.TOPK:\n\t\t\t// The heap keeps the lowest value on top, so reverse it.\n\t\t\tif len(aggr.heap) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse(aggr.heap))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, v := range aggr.heap {\n\t\t\t\tadd(v.Metric, v.F, v.H, v.DropName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.BOTTOMK:\n\t\t\t// The heap keeps the highest value on top, so reverse it.\n\t\t\tif len(aggr.heap) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\tsort.Sort(sort.Reverse((*vectorByReverseValueHeap)(&aggr.heap)))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfor _, v := range aggr.heap {\n\t\t\t\tadd(v.Metric, v.F, v.H, v.DropName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\tcase parser.LIMITK, parser.LIMIT_RATIO:\n\t\t\tfor _, v := range aggr.heap {\n\t\t\t\tadd(v.Metric, v.F, v.H, v.DropName)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn mat, annos\n}\n\n// aggregationCountValues evaluates count_values on vec.\n// Outputs as many series per group as there are values in the input.\nfunc (*evaluator) aggregationCountValues(e *parser.AggregateExpr, grouping []string, valueLabel string, vec Vector, enh *EvalNodeHelper) (Vector, annotations.Annotations) {\n\ttype groupCount struct {\n\t\tlabels labels.Labels\n\t\tcount  int\n\t}\n\tresult := map[uint64]*groupCount{}\n\n\tvar buf []byte\n\tfor _, s := range vec {\n\t\tenh.resetBuilder(s.Metric)\n\t\tif s.H == nil {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Set(valueLabel, strconv.FormatFloat(s.F, 'f', -1, 64))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tenh.lb.Set(valueLabel, s.H.String())\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetric := enh.lb.Labels()\n\n\t\t// Considering the count_values()\n\t\t// operator is less frequently used than other aggregations, we're fine having to\n\t\t// re-compute the grouping key on each step for this case.\n\t\tvar groupingKey uint64\n\t\tgroupingKey, buf = generateGroupingKey(metric, grouping, e.Without, buf)\n\n\t\tgroup, ok := result[groupingKey]\n\t\t// Add a new group if it doesn't exist.\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tresult[groupingKey] = &groupCount{\n\t\t\t\tlabels: generateGroupingLabels(enh, metric, e.Without, grouping),\n\t\t\t\tcount:  1,\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tgroup.count++\n\t}\n\n\t// Construct the result Vector from the aggregated groups.\n\tfor _, aggr := range result {\n\t\tenh.Out = shoudlWrap is false for cases like MatrixSelector and StringLiteral that never need to be wrapped.\nfunc preprocessExprHelper(expr parser.Expr, start, end time.Time) (isStepInvariant, shouldWrap bool) && argIsStepInvariant\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif isStepInvariant {\n\t\t\t// The function and all arguments are step invariant.\n\t\t\treturn true, true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor i, isi := range shouldWrap {\n\t\t\tif nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) query(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewInstantQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), ts)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\n\t// From now result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) formatQuery(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{expr.Pretty(0), nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) parseQuery(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{data: translateAST(expr), err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc extractQueryOpts(r *http.Request) (promql.QueryOpts, error) {\n\tvar duration time.Duration\n\n\tif strDuration := *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryExemplars(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start timestamp\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tselectors := parser.ExtractSelectors(expr)\n\tif len(selectors) < 1 {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, nil, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\teq, err := api.ExemplarQueryable.ExemplarQuerier(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tres, err := eq.Select(timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), selectors...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc returnAPIError(err error) *apiError {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar eqc promql.ErrQueryCanceled\n\tvar eqt promql.ErrQueryTimeout\n\tvar es promql.ErrStorage\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqc):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqt):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorTimeout, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &es):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorInternal, err}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &apiError{errorExec, err}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) labelNames(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit, err := TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rulesAlerts []*rules.Alert) []*Alert {\n\tapiAlerts := make([]*Alert, len(rulesAlerts))\n\tfor i, ruleAlert := range rulesAlerts {\n\t\tapiAlerts[i] = &Alert{\n\t\t\tLabels:      ruleAlert.Labels,\n\t\t\tAnnotations: ruleAlert.Annotations,\n\t\t\tState:       ruleAlert.State.String(),\n\t\t\tActiveAt:    &ruleAlert.ActiveAt,\n\t\t\tValue:       strconv.FormatFloat(ruleAlert.Value, 'e', -1, 64),\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince.IsZero() {\n\t\t\tapiAlerts[i].KeepFiringSince = &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiAlerts\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) metricMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tmetrics := map[string]map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\n\tlimit := -1\n\tif s := r.FormValue(\"limit\"); s != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif limit, err = strconv.Atoi(s); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New(\"limit must be a number\")}, nil, nil}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tlimitPerMetric := -1\n\tif s := r.FormValue(\"limit_per_metric\"); s != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tif limitPerMetric, err = strconv.Atoi(s); err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New(\"limit_per_metric must be a number\")}, nil, nil}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tmetric := r.FormValue(\"metric\")\n\tfor _, tt := range api.targetRetriever(r.Context()).TargetsActive() {\n\t\tfor _, t := range tt {\n\t\t\tif metric == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tfor _, mm := range t.ListMetadata() {\n\t\t\t\t\tm := metadata.Metadata{Type: mm.Type, Help: mm.Help, Unit: mm.Unit}\n\t\t\t\t\tms, ok := metrics[mm.MetricFamily]\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif limitPerMetric > 0 && len(ms) >= limitPerMetric {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tms = map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\t\tmetrics[mm.MetricFamily] = ms\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\tms[m] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif md, ok := t.GetMetadata(metric); ok {\n\t\t\t\tm := metadata.Metadata{Type: md.Type, Help: md.Help, Unit: md.Unit}\n\t\t\t\tms, ok := metrics[md.MetricFamily]\n\n\t\t\t\tif limitPerMetric > 0 && len(ms) >= limitPerMetric {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tms = map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics[md.MetricFamily] = ms\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tms[m] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Put the elements from the pseudo-set into a slice for marshaling.\n\tres := map[string][]metadata.Metadata{}\n\tfor name, set := range metrics {\n\t\tif limit >= 0 && len(res) >= limit {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ts := []metadata.Metadata{}\n\t\tfor metadata := range set {\n\t\t\ts = append(s, metadata)\n\t\t}\n\t\tres[name] = s\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// RuleDiscovery has info for all rules.\ntype RuleDiscovery struct {\n\tRuleGroups     []*RuleGroup `json:\"groups\"`\n\tGroupNextToken string       `json:\"groupNextToken,omitempty\"`\n}\n\n// RuleGroup has info for rules which are part of a group.\ntype RuleGroup struct {\n\tName string `json:\"name\"`\n\tFile string `json:\"file\"`\n\t// In order to preserve rule ordering, while exposing type (alerting or recording)\n\t// specific properties, both alerting and recording rules are exposed in the\n\t// same array.\n\tRules          []Rule    `json:\"rules\"`\n\tInterval       float64   `json:\"interval\"`\n\tLimit          int       `json:\"limit\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64   `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n}\n\ntype Rule any\n\ntype AlertingRule struct {\n\t// State can be \"pending\", \"firing\", \"inactive\".\n\tState          string           `json:\"state\"`\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tDuration       float64          `json:\"duration\"`\n\tKeepFiringFor  float64          `json:\"keepFiringFor\"`\n\tLabels         labels.Labels    `json:\"labels\"`\n\tAnnotations    labels.Labels    `json:\"annotations\"`\n\tAlerts         []*Alert         `json:\"alerts\"`\n\tHealth         rules.RuleHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\tLastError      string           `json:\"lastError,omitempty\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64          `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of an alertingRule is always \"alerting\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\ntype RecordingRule struct {\n\tName           string           `json:\"name\"`\n\tQuery          string           `json:\"query\"`\n\tLabels         labels.Labels    `json:\"labels,omitempty\"`\n\tHealth         rules.RuleHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\tLastError      string           `json:\"lastError,omitempty\"`\n\tEvaluationTime float64          `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\truleGroups := api.rulesRetriever(r.Context()).RuleGroups()\n\tres := &RuleDiscovery{RuleGroups: make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))}\n\ttyp := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"type\"))\n\n\tif typ != \"\" && typ != \"alert\" && typ != \"record\" {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"not supported value %q\", typ), \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := make([]*RuleGroup, 0, len(ruleGroups))\n\n\tfoundToken := false\n\n\tfor _, grp := range ruleGroups {\n\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\t\tif nextToken != getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := strings.ToLower(r.URL.Query().Get(\"exclude_alerts\"))\n\n\tif excludeAlertsParam == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := strconv.ParseBool(excludeAlertsParam)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"error converting exclude_alerts: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn excludeAlerts, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r *http.Request) (int64, string, *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the groups\"), \"group_next_token\")\n\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups != \"\" {\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups, err = strconv.ParseInt(maxGroups, 10, 32)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, nextToken, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn -1, \"\", nil\n}\n\nfunc getRuleGroupNextToken(file, group string) string {\n\th := sha1.New()\n\th.Write([]byte(file + \";\" + group))\n\treturn hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/event-stream\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Connection\", \"keep-alive\")\n\n\t// Subscribe to notifications.\n\tnotifications, unsubscribe, ok := api.notificationsSub()\n\tif !ok {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer unsubscribe()\n\n\t// Set up a flusher to push the response to the client.\n\tflusher, ok := w.(http.Flusher)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Streaming unsupported\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Flush the response to ensure the headers are immediately and eventSource\n\t// onopen is triggered client-side.\n\tflusher.Flush()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase notification := <-notifications:\n\t\t\t// Marshal the notification to JSON.\n\t\t\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(notification)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Write the event data in SSE format with JSON content.\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"data: %s\\n\\n\", jsonData)\n\n\t\t\t// Flush the response to ensure the data is sent immediately.\n\t\t\tflusher.Flush()\n\t\tcase <-r.Context().Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) remoteRead(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t// This is only really for tests - this will never be nil IRL.\n\tif deleteSeries(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif !api.enableAdmin {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New(\"admin APIs disabled\")}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tif err := by the caller) or call q.Close ourselves (which is required\n\t// in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tq.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\tcloser := func() {\n\t\tq.Close()\n\t}\n\n\thints := &storage.SelectHints{\n\t\tStart: timestamp.FromTime(start),\n\t\tEnd:   timestamp.FromTime(end),\n\t\tFunc:  \"series\", // There is no series function, this token is used for lookups that don't need samples.\n\t\tLimit: toHintLimit(limit),\n\t}\n\tvar set storage.SeriesSet\n\n\tif len(matcherSets) > 1 {\n\t\tvar sets []storage.SeriesSet\n\t\tfor _, mset := range matcherSets {\n\t\t\t// We need to sort this select results to merge (deduplicate) the series sets later.\n\t\t\ts := q.Select(ctx, true, hints, mset...)\n\t\t\tsets = append(sets, s)\n\t\t}\n\t\tset = storage.NewMergeSeriesSet(sets, 0, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// At this point at least one match exists.\n\t\tset = q.Select(ctx, false, hints, matcherSets[0]...)\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics := []labels.Labels{}\n\n\twarnings := set.Warnings()\n\n\ti := 1\n\tfor set.Next() {\n\t\tif i%checkContextEveryNIterations == 0 {\n\t\t\tif err := ctx.Err(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), warnings, closer}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\ti++\n\n\t\tmetrics = append(metrics, set.At().Labels())\n\n\t\tif limit > 0 && len(metrics) > limit {\n\t\t\tmetrics = metrics[:limit]\n\t\t\twarnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif set.Err() != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(set.Err()), warnings, closer}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{metrics, nil, warnings, closer}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) dropSeries(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, errors.New(\"not implemented\")}, nil, nil}\n}\n\n// Target has the information for one target.\ntype Target struct {\n\t// Labels before any processing.\n\tDiscoveredLabels labels.Labels `json:\"discoveredLabels\"`\n\t// Any labels that are added to this target and its metrics.\n\tLabels labels.Labels `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string              `json:\"lastError\"`\n\tLastScrape         time.Time           `json:\"lastScrape\"`\n\tLastScrapeDuration float64             `json:\"lastScrapeDuration\"`\n\tHealth             scrape.TargetHealth `json:\"health\"`\n\n\tScrapeInterval string `json:\"scrapeInterval\"`\n\tScrapeTimeout  string `json:\"scrapeTimeout\"`\n}\n\ntype ScrapePoolsDiscovery struct {\n\tScrapePools []string `json:\"scrapePools\"`\n}\n\n// DroppedTarget has the information for one target that was dropped during relabelling.\ntype DroppedTarget struct {\n\t// Labels before any processing.\n\tDiscoveredLabels labels.Labels `json:\"discoveredLabels\"`\n\tScrapePool       string        `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n}\n\n// TargetDiscovery has all the active targets.\ntype TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres :=   globalURL.String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError: func() string {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tswitch {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err == nil && lastErrStr == \"\":\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\treturn \"\"\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcase err != {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName:           grp.Name(),\n\t\t\tFile:           grp.File(),\n\t\t\tInterval:       grp.Interval().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLimit:          grp.Limit(),\n\t\t\tRules:          []Rule{},\n\t\t\tEvaluationTime: grp.GetEvaluationTime().Seconds(),\n\t\t\tLastEvaluation: grp.GetLastEvaluation(),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor _, rr := range grp.Rules(matcherSets...) {\n\t\t\tvar enrichedRule Rule\n\n\t\t\tif len(rnSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif _, ok := rnSet[rr.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tlastError := \"\"\n\t\t\tif rr.LastError() != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlastError = rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts     \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName: \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := string is needed to get the position information for the annotations, and it\n// can be empty if the position information isn't needed.\nfunc (api *API) respond(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request, data any, warnings annotations.Annotations, query string) {\n\tstatusMessage := statusSuccess\n\twarn, info := warnings.AsStrings(query, 10, 10)\n\n\tresp := &Response{\n\t\tStatus:   statusMessage,\n\t\tData:     data,\n\t\tWarnings: warn,\n\t\tInfos:    info,\n\t}\n\n\tcodec, err := api.negotiateCodec(req, resp)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.respondError(w, &apiError{errorNotAcceptable, err}, nil)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tb, err := codec.Encode(resp)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error marshaling response\", \"url\", req.URL, \"err\", err)\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", codec.ContentType().String())\n\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)\n\tif n, err := w.Write(b); err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error writing response\", \"url\", req.URL, \"bytesWritten\", n, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) negotiateCodec(req *http.Request, resp *Response) (Codec, error) {\n\tfor _, clause := range goautoneg.ParseAccept(req.Header.Get(\"Accept\")) {\n\t\tfor _, codec := range api.codecs {\n\t\t\tif codec.ContentType().Satisfies(clause) && codec.CanEncode(resp) {\n\t\t\t\treturn codec, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tdefaultCodec := api.codecs[0]\n\tif !defaultCodec.CanEncode(resp) {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot encode response as %s\", defaultCodec.ContentType())\n\t}\n\n\treturn defaultCodec, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) respondError(w http.ResponseWriter, apiErr *apiError, data any) {\n\tjson := jsoniter.ConfigCompatibleWithStandardLibrary\n\tb, err := json.Marshal(&Response{\n\t\tStatus:    statusError,\n\t\tErrorType: apiErr.typ.str,\n\t\tError:     apiErr.err.Error(),\n\t\tData:      data,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error marshaling json response\", \"err\", err)\n\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tvar code w.Write(b); err != nil {\n\t\tapi.logger.Error(\"error writing response\", \"bytesWritten\", n, \"err\", err)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc getDefaultErrorCode(errType errorType) int {\n\tswitch errType {\n\tcase errorBadData:\n\t\treturn http.StatusBadRequest\n\tcase errorExec:\n\t\treturn http.StatusUnprocessableEntity\n\tcase errorCanceled:\n\t\treturn statusClientClosedConnection\n\tcase errorTimeout:\n\t\treturn http.StatusServiceUnavailable\n\tcase errorInternal:\n\t\treturn http.StatusInternalServerError\n\tcase errorNotFound:\n\t\treturn http.StatusNotFound\n\tcase errorNotAcceptable:\n\t\treturn http.StatusNotAcceptable\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn http.StatusInternalServerError\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc parseTimeParam(r *http.Request, paramName string, defaultValue time.Time) (time.Time, error) {\n\tval := r.FormValue(paramName)\n\tif val == \"\" {\n\t\treturn defaultValue, nil\n\t}\n\tresult, err := parseTime(val)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid time value for '%s': %w\", paramName, err)\n\t}\n\treturn result, nil\n}\n\nfunc parseTime(s string) (time.Time, error) {\n\tif t, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {\n\t\ts, ns := math.Modf(t)\n\t\tns = math.Round(ns*1000) / 1000\n\t\treturn time.Unix(int64(s), int64(ns*float64(time.Second))).UTC(), nil\n\t}\n\tif t, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339Nano, s); err == nil {\n\t\treturn t, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Stdlib's time parser can only handle 4 digit years. As a workaround until\n\t// that is fixed we want to at least support our own boundary times.\n\t// Context: https://github.com/prometheus/client_golang/issues/614\n\t// Upstream issue: https://github.com/golang/go/issues/20555\n\tswitch s {\n\tcase minTimeFormatted:\n\t\treturn MinTime, nil\n\tcase maxTimeFormatted:\n\t\treturn MaxTime, nil\n\t}\n\treturn time.Time{}, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid timestamp\", s)\n}\n\nfunc parseDuration(s string) (time.Duration, error) {\n\tif d, err := strconv.ParseFloat(s, 64); err == nil {\n\t\tts := d * float64(time.Second)\n\t\tif ts > float64(math.MaxInt64) || ts < float64(math.MinInt64) {\n\t\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"cannot parse %q to a valid duration.                chan struct{}\n\tdone                 chan struct{}\n\trestored             bool\n\trestoreNewRuleGroups bool\n\n\tlogger *slog.Logger\n}\n\n// NotifyFunc sends notifications about a set of alerts generated by the given expression.\ntype NotifyFunc func(ctx context.Context, expr string, alerts ...*Alert)\n\n// ManagerOptions bundles options for the Manager.\ntype ManagerOptions It is blocking.\nfunc (m *Manager) Run() {\n\tm.logger.Info(\"Starting rule manager...\")\n\tm.start()\n\t<-m.done\n}\n\nfunc (m *Manager) start() {\n\tclose(m.block)\n}\n\n// Stop the rule manager's rule evaluation cycles.\nfunc (m *Manager) Stop() {\n\tm.mtx.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mtx.Unlock()\n\n\tm.logger.Info(\"Stopping rule manager...\")\n\n\t// Stop all groups asynchronously, then wait for them to finish.\n\t// This is faster than stopping and waiting for each group in sequence.\n\tfor _, eg := range m.groups {\n\t\teg.stopAsync()\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, eg := range m.groups {\n\t\teg.waitStopped()\n\t}\n\n\t// Shut down the groups waiting multiple evaluation intervals to write\n\t// staleness markers.\n\tclose(m.done)\n\n\tm.logger.Info(\"Rule manager stopped\")\n}\n\n// Update the rule manager's state as the config requires. If\n// loading the new rules failed the old rule set is restored.\n// This method will no-op in case the manager is already stopped.\nfunc (m *Manager) Update(interval time.Duration, files []string, externalLabels labels.Labels, externalURL string, groupEvalIterationFunc GroupEvalIterationFunc) error {\n\tm.mtx.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mtx.Unlock()\n\n\t// We cannot update a stopped manager\n\tselect {\n\tcase <-m.done:\n\t\treturn nil\n\tdefault:\n\t}\n\n\tgroups, errs := m.LoadGroups(interval, externalLabels, externalURL, groupEvalIterationFunc, false, files...)\n\n\tif errs != nil {\n\t\tfor _, e := range errs {\n\t\t\tm.logger.Error(\"loading groups failed\", \"err\", e)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn errors.New(\"error loading rules, previous rule set restored\")\n\t}\n\tm.restored = true\n\n\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n\tfor _, newg := range groups {\n\t\t// If there is an old group with the same identifier,\n\t\t// check if new group equals with the old group, if yes then skip it.\n\t\t// If not equals, stop it and wait for it to finish the current iteration.\n\t\t// Then copy it into the new group.\n\t\tgn := GroupKey(newg.file, newg.name)\n\t\toldg, ok := m.groups[gn]\n\t\tdelete(m.groups, gn)\n\n\t\tif ok && oldg.Equals(newg) {\n\t\t\tgroups[gn] = oldg\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\twg.Add(1)\n\t\tgo func(newg *Group) {\n\t\t\tif ok {\n\t\t\t\toldg.stop()\n\t\t\t\tnewg.CopyState(oldg)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\twg.Done()\n\t\t\t// Wait with starting evaluation until the rule manager\n\t\t\t// is told to run. (*rulefmt.RuleGroups, []error) {\n\treturn rulefmt.ParseFile(identifier, ignoreUnknownFields, nameValidationScheme)\n}\n\nfunc (FileLoader) Parse(query string) (parser.Expr, error) { return {\n\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t}\n\t\tt.cmds = append(t.cmds, cmd)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// testCommand is an interface that ensures that only the package internal\n// types can be a valid command for a map[uint64][]exemplar.Exemplar\n\twithNHCB  bool\n}\n\nfunc newLoadCmd(gap time.Duration, withNHCB bool) *loadCmd {\n\treturn &loadCmd{\n\t\tgap:       gap,\n\t\tmetrics: custom bounds and append them to the storage.\n\tfor _, histogramWrapper := range histogramMap {\n\t\tsamples := make([]promql.Sample, 0, len(histogramWrapper.histogramByTs))\n\t\tfor t, histogram := range histogramWrapper.histogramByTs {\n\t\t\th, fh, err := histogram.Convert()\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif fh == nil {\n\t\t\t\tif err := h.Validate(); err != nil string\n\texpectedFailRegexp        *regexp.Regexp\n\n\texpectedCmds map[expectCmdType][]expectCmd\n\n\tmetrics      map[uint64]labels.Labels\n\texpectScalar bool\n\texpected     map[uint64]entry\n}\n\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) isOrdered() bool {\n\treturn ev.ordered || (len(ev.expectedCmds[Ordered]) > 0)\n}\n\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) isFail() bool {\n\treturn ev.fail || (len(ev.expectedCmds[Fail]) > 0)\n}\n\ntype expectCmdType byte\n\nconst (\n\tOrdered expectCmdType = iota\n\tFail\n\tWarn\n\tNoWarn\n\tInfo\n\tNoInfo\n)\n\nvar expectTypeStr = map[string]expectCmdType{\n\t\"fail\":    Fail,\n\t\"ordered\": Ordered,\n\t\"warn\":    Warn,\n\t\"no_warn\": NoWarn,\n\t\"info\":    Info,\n\t\"no_info\": NoInfo,\n}\n\ntype expectCmd struct {\n\tmessage string\n\tregex   *regexp.Regexp\n}\n\nfunc (e *expectCmd) CheckMatch(str string) bool {\n\tif e.regex == nil {\n\t\treturn e.message == str\n\t}\n\treturn e.regex.MatchString(str)\n}\n\nfunc (e *expectCmd) String() string {\n\tif e.regex == nil {\n\t\treturn e.message\n\t}\n\treturn e.regex.String()\n}\n\nfunc (e *expectCmd) Type() string {\n\tif e.regex == nil {\n\t\treturn \"message\"\n\t}\n\treturn \"pattern\"\n}\n\ntype entry struct {\n\tpos  int\n\tvals []parser.SequenceValue\n}\n\nfunc (e entry) String() string {\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%d: %s\", e.pos, e.vals)\n}\n\nfunc newInstantEvalCmd(expr string, start time.Time, line int) *evalCmd {\n\treturn &evalCmd{\n\t\texpr:  expr,\n\t\tstart: start,\n\t\tline: \"eval\"\n}\n\n// expect adds a sequence of values to the set of expected\n// results for the query.\nfunc (ev *evalCmd) expect(pos int, vals ...parser.SequenceValue) {\n\tev.expectScalar = true\n\tev.expected[0] = entry{pos: pos, vals: vals}\n}\n\n// expectMetric adds a new metric with a sequence of values to the set of expected\n// results for the query.\nfunc (ev *evalCmd)
